119        public void test0001() throws JavaScriptModelException {
120                IJavaScriptUnit sourceUnit = getCompilationUnit("Converter15" , "src", "test0001", "X.js"); //$NON-NLS-1$ //$NON-NLS-2$ //$NON-NLS-3$ //$NON-NLS-4$
121                char[] source = sourceUnit.getSource().toCharArray();
122                ASTNode result = runJLS3Conversion(sourceUnit, true, true);
123                assertTrue("Not a compilation unit", result.getNodeType() == ASTNode.JAVASCRIPT_UNIT);
124                JavaScriptUnit compilationUnit = (JavaScriptUnit) result;
125                assertProblemsSize(compilationUnit, 0);
126                List types = compilationUnit.types();
127                assertEquals("Wrong number of types", 1, types.size());
128                AbstractTypeDeclaration typeDeclaration = (AbstractTypeDeclaration) types.get(0);
129                assertEquals("wrong type", ASTNode.TYPE_DECLARATION, typeDeclaration.getNodeType());
130                TypeDeclaration typeDeclaration2 = (TypeDeclaration) typeDeclaration;
131                List modifiers = typeDeclaration2.modifiers();
132                assertEquals("Wrong number of modifiers", 1, modifiers.size());
133                Modifier modifier = (Modifier) modifiers.get(0);
134                checkSourceRange(modifier, "public", source);
135                
136                ASTNode node = getASTNode(compilationUnit, 0, 0);
137                assertEquals("Wrong type", ASTNode.FIELD_DECLARATION, node.getNodeType());
138                FieldDeclaration fieldDeclaration = (FieldDeclaration) node;
139                modifiers = fieldDeclaration.modifiers();
140                assertEquals("Wrong number of modifiers", 3, modifiers.size());
141                modifier = (Modifier) modifiers.get(0);
142                checkSourceRange(modifier, "public", source);
143                modifier = (Modifier) modifiers.get(1);
144                checkSourceRange(modifier, "static", source);
145                modifier = (Modifier) modifiers.get(2);
146                checkSourceRange(modifier, "final", source);
147                
148                node = getASTNode(compilationUnit, 0, 1);
149                assertEquals("Wrong type", ASTNode.FUNCTION_DECLARATION, node.getNodeType());
150                FunctionDeclaration methodDeclaration = (FunctionDeclaration) node;
151                modifiers = methodDeclaration.modifiers();
152                assertEquals("Wrong number of modifiers", 2, modifiers.size());
153                modifier = (Modifier) modifiers.get(0);
154                checkSourceRange(modifier, "private", source);
155                modifier = (Modifier) modifiers.get(1);
156                checkSourceRange(modifier, "static", source);
157                List parameters = methodDeclaration.parameters();
158                assertEquals("Wrong number of parameters", 1, parameters.size());
159                SingleVariableDeclaration variableDeclaration = (SingleVariableDeclaration) parameters.get(0);
160                modifiers = variableDeclaration.modifiers();
161                assertEquals("Wrong number of modifiers", 1, modifiers.size());
162                modifier = (Modifier) modifiers.get(0);
163                checkSourceRange(modifier, "final", source);
164                
165                node = getASTNode(compilationUnit, 0, 2);
166                assertEquals("Wrong type", ASTNode.FUNCTION_DECLARATION, node.getNodeType());
167                methodDeclaration = (FunctionDeclaration) node;
168                modifiers = methodDeclaration.modifiers();
169                assertEquals("Wrong number of modifiers", 2, modifiers.size());
170                modifier = (Modifier) modifiers.get(0);
171                checkSourceRange(modifier, "public", source);
172                modifier = (Modifier) modifiers.get(1);
173                checkSourceRange(modifier, "static", source);
174        }

185        public void test0007() throws JavaScriptModelException {
186                IJavaScriptUnit sourceUnit = getCompilationUnit("Converter15" , "src", "test0007", "X.js"); //$NON-NLS-1$ //$NON-NLS-2$ //$NON-NLS-3$ //$NON-NLS-4$
187                char[] source = sourceUnit.getSource().toCharArray();
188                ASTNode result = runConversion(AST.JLS3, sourceUnit, true);
189                assertTrue("Not a compilation unit", result.getNodeType() == ASTNode.JAVASCRIPT_UNIT);
190                JavaScriptUnit compilationUnit = (JavaScriptUnit) result;
191                assertProblemsSize(compilationUnit, 0);
192                List imports = compilationUnit.imports();
193                assertEquals("Wrong size", 2, imports.size());
194                ImportDeclaration importDeclaration = (ImportDeclaration) imports.get(0);
195                checkSourceRange(importDeclaration, "import java.util.*;", source);
196                assertFalse("is static", importDeclaration.isStatic());
197                importDeclaration = (ImportDeclaration) imports.get(1);
198                checkSourceRange(importDeclaration, "import static java.io.File.*;", source);
199                assertTrue("not static", importDeclaration.isStatic());
200        }

216                IJavaScriptUnit sourceUnit = getCompilationUnit("Converter15" , "src", "test0009", "X.js"); //$NON-NLS-1$ //$NON-NLS-2$ //$NON-NLS-3$ //$NON-NLS-4$

234                checkSourceRange(expression, "args", source);
235                Statement body = enhancedForStatement.getBody();
236                checkSourceRange(body, "{System.out.println(s);}", source);
237        }

328                assertTrue("Not a compilation unit", result.getNodeType() == ASTNode.JAVASCRIPT_UNIT);
329                JavaScriptUnit compilationUnit = (JavaScriptUnit) result;
330                assertProblemsSize(compilationUnit, 0);
331                ASTNode node = getASTNode(compilationUnit, 0);
332                assertTrue("Not a type declaration", node.getNodeType() == ASTNode.TYPE_DECLARATION);
333                TypeDeclaration typeDeclaration = (TypeDeclaration) node;
334                SimpleName name = typeDeclaration.getName();
335                assertEquals("Wrong name", "Convertible", name.getIdentifier());
336                checkSourceRange(name, "Convertible", source);
337                List typeParameters = typeDeclaration.typeParameters();
338                assertEquals("Wrong size", 1, typeParameters.size());
339                TypeParameter typeParameter = (TypeParameter) typeParameters.get(0);
340                checkSourceRange(typeParameter, "T", source);
341                checkSourceRange(typeParameter.getName(), "T", source);
342                node = getASTNode(compilationUnit, 1);
343                assertTrue("Not a type declaration", node.getNodeType() == ASTNode.TYPE_DECLARATION);
344                typeDeclaration = (TypeDeclaration) node;
345                name = typeDeclaration.getName();
346                assertEquals("Wrong name", "X", name.getIdentifier());
347                checkSourceRange(name, "X", source);
348                typeParameters = typeDeclaration.typeParameters();
349                assertEquals("Wrong size", 2, typeParameters.size());
350                typeParameter = (TypeParameter) typeParameters.get(0);
351                checkSourceRange(typeParameter.getName(), "A", source);
352                checkSourceRange(typeParameter, "A extends Convertible<B>", source);
353                typeParameter = (TypeParameter) typeParameters.get(1);
354                checkSourceRange(typeParameter.getName(), "B", source);
355                checkSourceRange(typeParameter, "B extends Convertible<A>", source);
356                List typeBounds = typeParameter.typeBounds();
357                assertEquals("Wrong size", 1, typeBounds.size());
358                Type typeBound = (Type) typeBounds.get(0);
359                checkSourceRange(typeBound, "Convertible<A>", source);
360                assertEquals("wrong type", ASTNode.PARAMETERIZED_TYPE, typeBound.getNodeType());
361                ParameterizedType parameterizedType = (ParameterizedType) typeBound;
362                List typeArguments = parameterizedType.typeArguments();
363                assertEquals("Wrong size", 1, typeArguments.size());
364                Type typeArgument = (Type) typeArguments.get(0);
365                checkSourceRange(typeArgument, "A", source);
366        }

446        public void test0017() throws JavaScriptModelException {
447                IJavaScriptUnit sourceUnit = getCompilationUnit("Converter15" , "src", "test0017", "X.js"); //$NON-NLS-1$ //$NON-NLS-2$ //$NON-NLS-3$ //$NON-NLS-4$
448                ASTNode result = runJLS3Conversion(sourceUnit, true, true);
449                char[] source = sourceUnit.getSource().toCharArray();
450                assertTrue("Not a compilation unit", result.getNodeType() == ASTNode.JAVASCRIPT_UNIT);
451                JavaScriptUnit compilationUnit = (JavaScriptUnit) result;
452                assertProblemsSize(compilationUnit, 0);
453                ASTNode node = getASTNode(compilationUnit, 1, 0, 0);
454                assertTrue("Not a variable declaration statement", node.getNodeType() == ASTNode.VARIABLE_DECLARATION_STATEMENT);
455                VariableDeclarationStatement statement = (VariableDeclarationStatement) node;
456                List fragments = statement.fragments();
457                assertEquals("Wrong size", 1,  fragments.size());
458                VariableDeclarationFragment fragment = (VariableDeclarationFragment) fragments.get(0);
459                Expression initializer  = fragment.getInitializer();
460                assertNotNull("No initializer", initializer);
461                ITypeBinding binding = initializer.resolveTypeBinding();
462                assertNotNull("No binding", binding);
463                Type type = statement.getType();
464                assertTrue("Not a parameterized type", type.getNodeType() == ASTNode.PARAMETERIZED_TYPE);
465                ParameterizedType parameterizedType = (ParameterizedType) type;
466                List typeArguments = parameterizedType.typeArguments();
467                assertEquals("wrong size", 1, typeArguments.size());
468                Type typeArgument = (Type) typeArguments.get(0);
469                checkSourceRange(typeArgument, "Integer", source);
470                Type innerType = parameterizedType.getType();
471                assertTrue("Not a qualified type", innerType.getNodeType() == ASTNode.QUALIFIED_TYPE);
472                QualifiedType qualifiedType = (QualifiedType) innerType;
473                checkSourceRange(qualifiedType.getName(), "B", source);
474                Type qualifier = qualifiedType.getQualifier();
475                checkSourceRange(qualifier, "test0017.A<String>", source);
476                assertTrue("Not a parameterized type", qualifier.getNodeType() == ASTNode.PARAMETERIZED_TYPE);
477                ParameterizedType parameterizedType2 = (ParameterizedType) qualifier;
478                typeArguments = parameterizedType2.typeArguments();
479                assertEquals("wrong size", 1, typeArguments.size());
480                typeArgument = (Type) typeArguments.get(0);
481                checkSourceRange(typeArgument, "String", source);
482                innerType = parameterizedType2.getType();
483                assertTrue("Not a simple type", innerType.getNodeType() == ASTNode.SIMPLE_TYPE);
484                SimpleType simpleType = (SimpleType) innerType;
485                checkSourceRange(simpleType, "test0017.A", source);
486                Name name = simpleType.getName();
487                assertTrue("Not a qualified name", name.getNodeType() == ASTNode.QUALIFIED_NAME);
488                QualifiedName qualifiedName = (QualifiedName) name;
489                checkSourceRange(qualifiedName.getQualifier(), "test0017", source);
490                checkSourceRange(qualifiedName.getName(), "A", source);                
491        }

641                FunctionDeclaration declaration = (FunctionDeclaration) node;
642                List parameters = declaration.parameters();
643                assertEquals("Wrong size", 1, parameters.size());
644                SingleVariableDeclaration singleVariableDeclaration = (SingleVariableDeclaration) parameters.get(0);
645                Type type = singleVariableDeclaration.getType();
646                assertTrue("Not a parameterized type", type.getNodeType() == ASTNode.PARAMETERIZED_TYPE);
647                ParameterizedType parameterizedType = (ParameterizedType) type;
648                List typeArguments = parameterizedType.typeArguments();
649                assertEquals("Wrong size", 1, typeArguments.size());
650                Type typeArgument = (Type) typeArguments.get(0);
651                checkSourceRange(typeArgument, "? super E", source);
652                assertTrue("Not a wildcard type", typeArgument.getNodeType() == ASTNode.WILDCARD_TYPE);
653                WildcardType wildcardType = (WildcardType) typeArgument;
654                Type bound = wildcardType.getBound();
655                checkSourceRange(bound, "E", source);
656                assertFalse("Is an upper bound", wildcardType.isUpperBound());
657        }

918                JavaScriptUnit compilationUnit = (JavaScriptUnit) result;
919                assertProblemsSize(compilationUnit, 0);

934                assertEquals("Wrong size", 0, typeParameters.length);
935                assertEquals("Wrong isArray", false, typeBinding.isArray());

948                assertEquals("Wrong isRawType", false, typeBinding.isRawType());

950                assertEquals("Wrong isUpperbound", false, typeBinding.isUpperbound());
951                assertEquals("Wrong isTypeVariable", true, typeBinding.isTypeVariable());
952                assertTrue("Not from source", typeBinding.isFromSource());
953                assertEquals("Wrong isWildcardType", false, typeBinding.isWildcardType());
954                ITypeBinding typeBinding2 = type.resolveBinding();
955                assertEquals("Wrong name", "X<T>", typeBinding2.getName());
956                assertEquals("Wrong isArray", false, typeBinding2.isArray());

958                assertEquals("Wrong isAnonymous", false, typeBinding2.isAnonymous());
959                assertEquals("Wrong isClass", true, typeBinding2.isClass());
960                assertEquals("Wrong isEnum", false, typeBinding2.isEnum());
961                assertEquals("Wrong isInterface", false, typeBinding2.isInterface());
962                assertEquals("Wrong isGenericType", false, typeBinding2.isGenericType());
963                assertEquals("Wrong isLocal", false, typeBinding2.isLocal());
964                assertEquals("Wrong isMember", false, typeBinding2.isMember());
965                assertEquals("Wrong isNested", false, typeBinding2.isNested());
966                assertEquals("Wrong isNullType", false, typeBinding2.isNullType());
967                assertEquals("Wrong isParameterizedType", true, typeBinding2.isParameterizedType());
968                assertEquals("Wrong isPrimitive", false, typeBinding2.isPrimitive());
969                assertEquals("Wrong isRawType", false, typeBinding2.isRawType());
970                assertEquals("Wrong isTopLevel", true, typeBinding2.isTopLevel());
971                assertEquals("Wrong isUpperbound", false, typeBinding2.isUpperbound());
972                assertEquals("Wrong isTypeVariable", false, typeBinding2.isTypeVariable());
973                assertEquals("Wrong isWildcardType", false, typeBinding2.isWildcardType());

976        }

1293        /*
1294         * Ensures that the type parameters of a method are included in its binding key.
1295         * (regression test for 73970 [1.5][dom] overloaded parameterized methods have same method binding key)
1296         */
1297        public void test0060() throws JavaScriptModelException {
1298                this.workingCopy = getWorkingCopy("/Converter15/src/p/X.js", true/*resolve*/);
1299                ASTNode node = buildAST(
1300                        "package p;\n" +
1301                        "/*start*/public class X {\n" +
1302                        "  <T> void foo(T t) {\n" +
1303                        "  }\n" +
1304                        "  <T extends X> void foo(T t) {\n" +
1305                        "  }\n" +
1306                        "  <T extends Class> void foo(T t) {\n" +
1307                        "  }\n" +
1308                        "  <T extends Exception & Runnable> void foo(T t) {\n" +
1309                        "  }\n" +
1310                        "}/*end*/",
1311                        this.workingCopy,
1312                        false);
1313                FunctionDeclaration[] methods = ((TypeDeclaration) node).getMethods();
1314                int length = methods.length;
1315                String[] keys = new String[length];
1316                for (int i = 0; i < length; i++)
1317                        keys[i] = methods[i].resolveBinding().getKey();
1318                assertBindingKeysEqual(
1319                        "Lp/X;.foo<T:Ljava/lang/Object;>(TT;)V\n" + 
1320                        "Lp/X;.foo<T:Lp/X;>(TT;)V\n" + 
1321                        "Lp/X;.foo<T:Ljava/lang/Class;>(TT;)V\n" + 
1322                        "Lp/X;.foo<T:Ljava/lang/Exception;:Ljava/lang/Runnable;>(TT;)V",
1323                        keys);
1324        }
1325 
1326        /*
1327         * Ensures that the type parameters of a generic type are included in its binding key.
1328         * (regression test for 77808 [1.5][dom] type bindings for raw List and List<E> have same key)
1329         */
1330        public void test0061() throws JavaScriptModelException {

1333                        "package p;\n" +
1334                        "/*start*/public class X<T> {\n" +
1335                        "}/*end*/",
1336                        this.workingCopy);
1337                IBinding binding = ((TypeDeclaration) node).resolveBinding();
1338                assertBindingKeyEquals(
1339                        "Lp/X<TT;>;",
1340                        binding.getKey());
1341        }

1363        public void test0063() throws JavaScriptModelException {
1364                IJavaScriptUnit sourceUnit = getCompilationUnit("Converter15" , "src", "test0063", "X.js"); //$NON-NLS-1$ //$NON-NLS-2$ //$NON-NLS-3$ //$NON-NLS-4$
1365                ASTNode result = runJLS3Conversion(sourceUnit, true, false);
1366                assertNotNull(result);
1367                assertTrue("Not a compilation unit", result.getNodeType() == ASTNode.JAVASCRIPT_UNIT);
1368                JavaScriptUnit compilationUnit = (JavaScriptUnit) result;
1369                assertProblemsSize(compilationUnit, 0);
1370                ASTNode node = getASTNode(compilationUnit, 0);
1371                assertEquals("Wrong node", ASTNode.TYPE_DECLARATION, node.getNodeType());
1372                TypeDeclaration typeDeclaration = (TypeDeclaration) node;
1373                ITypeBinding typeBinding = typeDeclaration.resolveBinding();
1374                assertNotNull("No binding", typeBinding);
1375                assertEquals("Wrong qualified name", "test0063.X", typeBinding.getQualifiedName());
1376                node = getASTNode(compilationUnit, 0, 0, 0);
1377                assertEquals("Wrong node", ASTNode.RETURN_STATEMENT, node.getNodeType());
1378                ReturnStatement returnStatement = (ReturnStatement) node;
1379                Expression expression = returnStatement.getExpression();
1380                typeBinding = expression.resolveTypeBinding();
1381                assertTrue("Not parameterized", typeBinding.isParameterizedType());
1382                assertEquals("Wrong qualified name", "test0063.X<java.lang.String>", typeBinding.getQualifiedName());                
1383                node = getASTNode(compilationUnit, 0, 1);
1384                assertEquals("Wrong node", ASTNode.FUNCTION_DECLARATION, node.getNodeType());
1385                FunctionDeclaration methodDeclaration = (FunctionDeclaration) node;
1386                List parameters = methodDeclaration.parameters();
1387                assertEquals("Wrong size", 1, parameters.size());
1388                SingleVariableDeclaration declaration = (SingleVariableDeclaration) parameters.get(0);
1389                Type type = declaration.getType();
1390                typeBinding = type.resolveBinding();
1391                assertEquals("Wrong qualified name", "java.util.List<? extends test0063.X<?>>", typeBinding.getQualifiedName());                                
1392        }

1626                assertTrue("Not a simple type", type4.isSimpleType());
1627                SimpleType simpleType = (SimpleType) type4;
1628                typeBinding = simpleType.resolveBinding();
1629                assertNotNull("No binding", typeBinding);

1631                Name name = simpleType.getName();

1663         * https://bugs.eclipse.org/bugs/show_bug.cgi?id=77645
1664         */
1665        public void test0072() throws JavaScriptModelException {
1666                IJavaScriptUnit sourceUnit = getCompilationUnit("Converter15", "src", "test0072", "X.js"); //$NON-NLS-1$ //$NON-NLS-2$ //$NON-NLS-3$ //$NON-NLS-4$
1667                ASTNode result = runConversion(AST.JLS3, sourceUnit, true);
1668                assertEquals("not a compilation unit", ASTNode.JAVASCRIPT_UNIT, result.getNodeType()); //$NON-NLS-1$
1669                JavaScriptUnit unit = (JavaScriptUnit) result;
1670                assertProblemsSize(unit, 0);
1671                unit.accept(new ASTVisitor() {
1672                        /* (non-Javadoc)
1673                         * @see org.eclipse.wst.jsdt.core.dom.ASTVisitor#visit(org.eclipse.wst.jsdt.core.dom.SingleVariableDeclaration)
1674                         */
1675                        public boolean visit(SingleVariableDeclaration node) {
1676                                IVariableBinding binding = node.resolveBinding();
1677                                assertNotNull("No method", binding.getDeclaringMethod());
1678                                return false;
1679                        }
1680                        /* (non-Javadoc)
1681                         * @see org.eclipse.wst.jsdt.core.dom.ASTVisitor#visit(org.eclipse.wst.jsdt.core.dom.VariableDeclarationFragment)
1682                         */
1683                        public boolean visit(VariableDeclarationFragment node) {
1684                                IVariableBinding binding = node.resolveBinding();
1685                                ASTNode parent = node.getParent();
1686                                if (parent != null && binding != null) {
1687                                        final IFunctionBinding declaringMethod = binding.getDeclaringMethod();
1688                                        final String variableBindingName = binding.getName();
1689                                        switch(parent.getNodeType()) {
1690                                                case ASTNode.FIELD_DECLARATION :
1691                                                        assertNull("Got a method", declaringMethod);
1692                                                        break;
1693                                                default :
1694                                                        if (variableBindingName.equals("var1")
1695                                                                        || variableBindingName.equals("var2")) {
1696                                                                assertNull("Got a method", declaringMethod);
1697                                                        } else {
1698                                                                assertNotNull("No method", declaringMethod);
1699                                                                String methodName = declaringMethod.getName();
1700                                                                if (variableBindingName.equals("var4")) {
1701                                                                        assertEquals("Wrong method", "foo", methodName);
1702                                                                } else if (variableBindingName.equals("var5")) {
1703                                                                        assertEquals("Wrong method", "foo2", methodName);
1704                                                                } else if (variableBindingName.equals("var7")) {
1705                                                                        assertEquals("Wrong method", "foo3", methodName);
1706                                                                } else if (variableBindingName.equals("var8")) {
1707                                                                        assertEquals("Wrong method", "X", methodName);
1708                                                                } else if (variableBindingName.equals("var9")) {
1709                                                                        assertEquals("Wrong method", "bar3", methodName);
1710                                                                } else if (variableBindingName.equals("var10")) {
1711                                                                        assertEquals("Wrong method", "bar3", methodName);
1712                                                                } else if (variableBindingName.equals("var11")) {
1713                                                                        assertEquals("Wrong method", "bar3", methodName);
1714                                                                } else if (variableBindingName.equals("var12")) {
1715                                                                        assertEquals("Wrong method", "X", methodName);
1716                                                                } 
1717                                                        }
1718                                        }
1719                                }
1720                                return false;
1721                        }
1722                        /* (non-Javadoc)
1723                         * @see org.eclipse.wst.jsdt.core.dom.ASTVisitor#visit(org.eclipse.wst.jsdt.core.dom.FieldAccess)
1724                         */
1725                        public boolean visit(FieldAccess node) {
1726                                IVariableBinding binding = node.resolveFieldBinding();
1727                                assertNull("No method", binding.getDeclaringMethod());
1728                                return false;
1729                        }
1730                        /* (non-Javadoc)
1731                         * @see org.eclipse.wst.jsdt.core.dom.ASTVisitor#endVisit(org.eclipse.wst.jsdt.core.dom.SuperFieldAccess)
1732                         */
1733                        public boolean visit(SuperFieldAccess node) {
1734                                IVariableBinding binding = node.resolveFieldBinding();
1735                                assertNull("No method", binding.getDeclaringMethod());
1736                                return false;
1737                        }
1738                });
1739        }

2318                        }
2319                        /* (non-Javadoc)
2320                         * @see org.eclipse.wst.jsdt.core.dom.ASTVisitor#endVisit(org.eclipse.wst.jsdt.core.dom.SuperFieldAccess)
2321                         */
2322                        public boolean visit(SuperFieldAccess node) {
2323                                IVariableBinding binding = node.resolveFieldBinding();
2324                                assertNotNull("No binding", binding);
2325                                IJavaScriptElement javaElement = binding.getJavaElement();
2326                                assertNotNull("No java element", javaElement);
2327                                return false;
2328                        }
2329                });
2330        }

2882            "        }\n" +
2883            "}",
2884            this.workingCopy);

2898        statement = (ExpressionStatement) node;

2901        methodInvocation = (FunctionInvocation) expression;
2902        IFunctionBinding methodBinding2 = methodInvocation.resolveMethodBinding();
2903        assertFalse("Keys are equals", methodBinding.getKey().equals(methodBinding2.getKey()));
2904        assertFalse("bindings are equals", methodBinding.isEqualTo(methodBinding2));
2905    }

3001                "                Outer<String>.Inner.InnerInner<Integer> in = new Outer<String>().new Inner(). new InnerInner<Integer>();\n" +
3002                "        }\n" +
3003                "}";

3005            contents,
3006            this.workingCopy);

3018                assertNotNull("No binding", typeBinding);

3029                assertEquals("Wrong qualified name 3", "Outer<java.lang.String>.Inner.InnerInner<java.lang.Integer>", typeBinding.getQualifiedName());

3065                        "        public void bar(String... args){\n" +
3066                        "        }\n" +
3067                        "}";
3068             ASTNode node = buildAST(
3069                                contents,
3070                            this.workingCopy);
3071                   assertNotNull("No node", node);
3072            assertEquals("Not a compilation unit", ASTNode.JAVASCRIPT_UNIT, node.getNodeType());
3073            JavaScriptUnit compilationUnit = (JavaScriptUnit) node;
3074            assertProblemsSize(compilationUnit, 0);

3092            assertTrue("Not an array binding", parameterType.isArray());

3094            assertEquals("wrong dimension", 1, parameterType.getDimensions());

3098    public void test0132() throws CoreException {
3099            this.workingCopy = getWorkingCopy("/Converter15/src/X.js", true/*resolve*/);
3100            String contents =
3101                    "public class X {\n" +
3102                    "        public void bar(String[]... args[]){\n" +
3103                    "        }\n" +
3104                    "}";
3105            ASTNode node = buildAST(
3106                                contents,
3107                            this.workingCopy,
3108                            false);
3109            assertNotNull("No node", node);
3110            assertEquals("Not a compilation unit", ASTNode.JAVASCRIPT_UNIT, node.getNodeType());
3111            JavaScriptUnit compilationUnit = (JavaScriptUnit) node;
3112            assertProblemsSize(compilationUnit, 1, "Extended dimensions are illegal for a variable argument");
3113            node = getASTNode(compilationUnit, 0, 0);
3114            assertEquals("Not a method declaration", ASTNode.FUNCTION_DECLARATION, node.getNodeType());
3115            FunctionDeclaration methodDeclaration = (FunctionDeclaration) node;
3116            List parameters = methodDeclaration.parameters();
3117            assertEquals("Wrong size", 1, parameters.size());
3118            SingleVariableDeclaration singleVariableDeclaration = (SingleVariableDeclaration) parameters.get(0);
3119            assertTrue("Not a var args", singleVariableDeclaration.isVarargs());
3120                assertTrue("Not a malformed node", isMalformed(singleVariableDeclaration));
3121            Type type = singleVariableDeclaration.getType();
3122            checkSourceRange(type, "String[]", contents);
3123            assertTrue("Not an array type", type.isArrayType());
3124            ITypeBinding typeBinding = type.resolveBinding();
3125            assertNotNull("No binding", typeBinding);
3126            assertTrue("Not an array", typeBinding.isArray());
3127            assertEquals("wrong dimensions", 1, typeBinding.getDimensions());
3128            ArrayType arrayType = (ArrayType) type;
3129            assertEquals("Wrong dimension", 1, arrayType.getDimensions());
3130            type = arrayType.getComponentType();
3131            assertTrue("Not a simple type", type.isSimpleType());
3132            checkSourceRange(type, "String", contents);
3133            assertEquals("Wrong extra dimension", 1, singleVariableDeclaration.getExtraDimensions());
3134                IFunctionBinding methodBinding = methodDeclaration.resolveBinding();
3135                ITypeBinding[] parameterTypes = methodBinding.getParameterTypes();
3136                ITypeBinding parameterType = parameterTypes[0];
3137            assertTrue("Not an array binding", parameterType.isArray());
3138               assertEquals("wrong dimension", 3, parameterType.getDimensions());                
3139               ITypeBinding componentType = parameterType.getComponentType();

4173        /*

4175         * (regression test for bug 92888 ITypeBinding#isEqualTo(..) is wrong for capture bindings)
4176         */
4177        public void test0172() throws JavaScriptModelException {
4178            this.workingCopy = getWorkingCopy("/Converter15/src/X.js", true/*resolve*/);
4179            String contents =
4180                        "public class X<T> {\n" + 
4181                        "  private static X<? super Number> num() {\n" + 
4182                        "                return null;\n" + 
4183                        "        }\n" +
4184                        "  void add(T t) {\n" +
4185                        "  }\n" +
4186                        "  void foo() {\n" + 
4187                        "    Number n= null;\n" + 
4188                        "    /*start1*/num().add(null)/*end1*/;\n" + 
4189                        "    /*start2*/num().add(n)/*end2*/;\n" + 
4190                        "  }\n" +
4191                        "}\n";
4192                   IBinding[] bindings = resolveBindings(contents, this.workingCopy);
4193                   assertTrue("2 different capture bindings should not be equals", !bindings[0].isEqualTo(bindings[1]));

4313    public void test0178() throws CoreException {

4317                                "\n" +
4318                                "public class X {\n" +
4319                                "        void foo() {\n" +
4320                                "                Vector< ? super java.util.Collection<? super java.lang.Number> > lhs= null;                \n" +
4321                                "        }\n" +
4322                                "}";
4323                   ASTNode node = buildAST(
4324                                contents,
4325                            this.workingCopy);
4326                   assertEquals("Not a compilation unit", ASTNode.JAVASCRIPT_UNIT, node.getNodeType());
4327                   JavaScriptUnit unit = (JavaScriptUnit) node;

4336                   assertEquals("Wrong size", 1, typeArguments.size());
4337                   Type typeArgument = (Type) typeArguments.get(0);
4338                   assertEquals("Not a wildcard type", ASTNode.WILDCARD_TYPE, typeArgument.getNodeType());
4339                   WildcardType wildcardType = (WildcardType) typeArgument;
4340                   checkSourceRange(wildcardType, "? super java.util.Collection<? super java.lang.Number>", contents);
4341                   Type bound = wildcardType.getBound();
4342                   assertEquals("Not a parameterized type", ASTNode.PARAMETERIZED_TYPE, bound.getNodeType());
4343                   ParameterizedType parameterizedType2 = (ParameterizedType) bound;
4344                   checkSourceRange(bound, "java.util.Collection<? super java.lang.Number>", contents);
4345                   typeArguments = parameterizedType2.typeArguments();
4346                   assertEquals("Wrong size", 1, typeArguments.size());
4347                   typeArgument = (Type) typeArguments.get(0);
4348                   assertEquals("Not a wildcard type", ASTNode.WILDCARD_TYPE, typeArgument.getNodeType());
4349                   wildcardType = (WildcardType) typeArgument;
4350                   checkSourceRange(wildcardType, "? super java.lang.Number", contents);
4351    }

4685        // Wrong ParameterizedTypeBinding yields null type declaration result
4686        // https://bugs.eclipse.org/bugs/show_bug.cgi?id=100584
4687        public void test0192() throws JavaScriptModelException {
4688            this.workingCopy = getWorkingCopy("/Converter15/src/X.js", true/*resolve*/);
4689            String contents =
4690                        "public class X<E> {\n" + 
4691                        "        public static class InnerClass {\n" + 
4692                        "                static class InnerInnerClass {\n" + 
4693                        "                        /*start*/X.WrongInnerClass/*end*/.InnerInnerClass m;\n" + 
4694                        "                }\n" + 
4695                        "        }\n" + 
4696                        "}";
4697                   IBinding[] bindings = resolveBindings(contents, this.workingCopy, false/*don't report errors*/);
4698                   if (bindings[0] != null) {
4699                           // should not get here if patch 100584 applied
4700                           try {
4701                                   bindings[0].toString();
4702                                   fail("should get an exception if bug 100584 present");
4703                                   // which means that the code would now return a non null, 
4704                                   // erroneous binding, yet able to respond to toString
4705                           } catch (Throwable t) {/* absorb quietly */}
4706                   }
4707                   assertTrue("should yield a null, not a malformed binding", 
4708                                   bindings[0] == null);
4709        }

4831        /*

4833         * doesn't throw an NPE
4834         * (regression test for bug 100606 NPE during reconcile)
4835         */
4836        public void test0197() throws CoreException {
4837                try {
4838                        createJavaProject("P", new String[] {"src" }, new String[] {"CONVERTER_JCL15_LIB", "/P/lib"}, "bin", "1.5");
4839                        IFolder folder = createFolder("/P/lib");
4840                        String classesPath = folder.getLocation().toOSString();
4841                        Map options = new HashMap();
4842                        String[] pathsAndContents = new String[] {
4843                                "p/Bin.js",
4844                                "package p;\n" +
4845                                "public class Bin {\n" +
4846                                "}",
4847                                "p/BinSub.js",
4848                                "package p;\n" +
4849                                "public class BinSub extends Bin {\n" +
4850                                "}",
4851                        };
4852                        Util.compile(pathsAndContents, options, classesPath);
4853                        folder.refreshLocal(IResource.DEPTH_INFINITE, null);
4854//                        folder.getFolder("p").getFile("Bin.class").delete(false, null);
4855                        Util.delete(folder.getFolder("p").getFile("Bin.class"));
4856                    this.workingCopy = getWorkingCopy("/P/src/X.js", true/*resolve*/);
4857                    String contents =
4858                                "public class X {\n" + 
4859                                "        void bar() throws p.BinSub {\n" + 
4860                                "        }\n" + 
4861                                "        </*start*/T/*end*/> void foo() {\n" + 
4862                                "        }\n" + 
4863                                "}";
4864                           IBinding[] bindings = resolveBindings(contents, this.workingCopy, false/*don't report errors*/);
4865                           assertBindingsEqual(
4866                                   "LX;.foo<T:Ljava/lang/Object;>()V:TT;",
4867                                   bindings);
4868                } finally {
4869                        deleteProject("P");
4870                }
4871        }

5494                        "         \n" +

5763                        @interface Annot {
5764                                String message() default "";
5765                        }
5766                        
5767                        package test0233;
5768                        
5769                        @Annot(message="Hello, World!")
5770                        public class X {
5771                        }
5772                 */
5773                String contents =
5774                        "import test0233.X;\n" +
5775                        "public class A {\n" + 
5776                        "    X test() {\n" + 
5777                        "        return null;\n" + 
5778                        "    }\n" + 
5779                        "}";

5782                        contents,
5783                        workingCopy,
5784                        true);

5786                JavaScriptUnit unit = (JavaScriptUnit) node;
5787                assertProblemsSize(unit, 0);
5788                node = getASTNode(unit, 0, 0);

5791                Type type = declaration.getReturnType2();

6166                Type type = fieldDeclaration.getType();
6167                ITypeBinding typeBinding = type.resolveBinding();
6168                assertNotNull("No binding", typeBinding);
6169                IJavaScriptElement element = typeBinding.getJavaElement();
6170                assertNotNull("No element", element);
6171                assertTrue("Doesn't exist", element.exists());
6172                assertEquals("Wrong handle identifier", "=Converter15/src<xy{X.java[X[Inner", element.getHandleIdentifier());
6173        }
6174}
